err != nil {\n   239→\t\treturn nil, err\n   240→\t}\n   241→\n   242→\tvar paths []string\n   243→\tif err := fs.WalkDir(src, \".\", func(path string, d fs.DirEntry, err error) error {\n   244→\t\tif err != nil {\n   245→\t\t\treturn err\n   246→\t\t}\n   247→\n   248→\t\tif d.IsDir() {\n   249→\t\t\treturn nil\n   250→\t\t}\n   251→\n   252→\t\tif idx.Match(path) {\n   253→\t\t\tpaths = append(paths, path)\n   254→\t\t}\n   255→\n   256→\t\treturn nil\n   257→\t}); err != nil {\n   258→\t\treturn nil, err\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\treturn paths, nil\n   262→}\n   263→\n   264→func (ss *Snapshot) addDoc(doc *ext.Document) error {\n   265→\tns := ss.ns[doc.Namespace]\n   266→\tif ns == nil {\n   267→\t\tns = newNamespace(doc.Namespace, doc.Namespace, ss.now)\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\tevalDists := map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{}\n   271→\tif len(ss.evalDists) > 0 {\n   272→\t\tevalDists = ss.evalDists\n   273→\t}\n   274→\n   275→\tfor _, s := range doc.Segments {\n   276→\t\tmatchType := flipt.MatchType_value[s.MatchType]\n   277→\t\tsegment := &flipt.Segment{\n   278→\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   279→\t\t\tName:         s.Name,\n   280→\t\t\tKey:          s.Key,\n   281→\t\t\tDescription:  s.Description,\n   282→\t\t\tMatchType:    flipt.MatchType(matchType),\n   283→\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   284→\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   285→\t\t}\n   286→\n   287→\t\tfor _, constraint := range s.Constraints {\n   288→\t\t\tconstraintType := flipt.ComparisonType_value[constraint.Type]\n   289→\t\t\tsegment.Constraints = append(segment.Constraints, &flipt.Constraint{\n   290→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   291→\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:   segment.Key,\n   292→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   293→\t\t\t\tOperator:     constraint.Operator,\n   294→\t\t\t\tProperty:     constraint.Property,\n   295→\t\t\t\tType:         flipt.ComparisonType(constraintType),\n   296→\t\t\t\tValue:        constraint.Value,\n   297→\t\t\t\tDescription:  constraint.Description,\n   298→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   299→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   300→\t\t\t})\n   301→\t\t}\n   302→\n   303→\t\tns.segments[segment.Key] = segment\n   304→\t}\n   305→\n   306→\tfor _, f := range doc.Flags {\n   307→\t\tflagType := flipt.FlagType_value[f.Type]\n   308→\t\tflag := &flipt.Flag{\n   309→\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   310→\t\t\tKey:          f.Key,\n   311→\t\t\tName:         f.Name,\n   312→\t\t\tDescription:  f.Description,\n   313→\t\t\tEnabled:      f.Enabled,\n   314→\t\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType(flagType),\n   315→\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   316→\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   317→\t\t}\n   318→\n   319→\t\tfor _, v := range f.Variants {\n   320→\t\t\tattachment, err := json.Marshal(v.Attachment)\n   321→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   322→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   323→\t\t\t}\n   324→\n   325→\t\t\tflag.Variants = append(flag.Variants, &flipt.Variant{\n   326→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   327→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   328→\t\t\t\tKey:          v.Key,\n   329→\t\t\t\tName:         v.Name,\n   330→\t\t\t\tDescription:  v.Description,\n   331→\t\t\t\tAttachment:   string(attachment),\n   332→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   333→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   334→\t\t\t})\n   335→\t\t}\n   336→\n   337→\t\tns.flags[f.Key] = flag\n   338→\n   339→\t\tevalRules := []*storage.EvaluationRule{}\n   340→\t\tfor i, r := range f.Rules {\n   341→\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n   342→\t\t\trule := &flipt.Rule{\n   343→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   344→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   345→\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n   346→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   347→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   348→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   349→\t\t\t}\n   350→\n   351→\t\t\tevalRule := &storage.EvaluationRule{\n   352→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   353→\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n   354→\t\t\t\tID:           rule.Id,\n   355→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   356→\t\t\t}\n   357→\n   358→\t\t\tswitch s := r.Segment.IsSegment.(type) {\n   359→\t\t\tcase ext.SegmentKey:\n   360→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKey = string(s)\n   361→\t\t\tcase *ext.Segments:\n   362→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKeys = s.Keys\n   363→\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[s.SegmentOperator]\n   364→\n   365→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator)\n   366→\t\t\t}\n   367→\n   368→\t\t\tvar (\n   369→\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n   370→\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n   371→\t\t\t)\n   372→\n   373→\t\t\tif rule.SegmentKey != \"\" {\n   374→\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKey)\n   375→\t\t\t} else if len(rule.SegmentKeys) > 0 {\n   376→\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKeys...)\n   377→\t\t\t}\n   378→\n   379→\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n   380→\t\t\t\tsegment := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n   381→\t\t\t\tif segment == nil {\n   382→\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n   383→\t\t\t\t}\n   384→\n   385→\t\t\t\tevc := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n   386→\t\t\t\tfor _, constraint := range segment.Constraints {\n   387→\t\t\t\t\tevc = append(evc, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n   388→\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: constraint.Operator,\n   389→\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: constraint.Property,\n   390→\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     constraint.Type,\n   391→\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    constraint.Value,\n   392→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   393→\t\t\t\t}\n   394→\n   395→\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n   396→\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n   397→\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n   398→\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: evc,\n   399→\t\t\t\t}\n   400→\t\t\t}\n   401→\n   402→\t\t\tif rule.SegmentOperator == flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR {\n   403→\t\t\t\tevalRule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n   404→\t\t\t}\n   405→\n   406→\t\t\tevalRule.Segments = segments\n   407→\n   408→\t\t\tevalRules = append(evalRules, evalRule)\n   409→\n   410→\t\t\tfor _, d := range r.Distributions {\n   411→\t\t\t\tvariant, found := findByKey(d.VariantKey, flag.Variants...)\n   412→\t\t\t\tif !found {\n   413→\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown variant %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, d.VariantKey)\n   414→\t\t\t\t}\n   415→\n   416→\t\t\t\tid := uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String()\n   417→\t\t\t\trule.Distributions = append(rule.Distributions, &flipt.Distribution{\n   418→\t\t\t\t\tId:        id,\n   419→\t\t\t\t\tRollout:   d.Rollout,\n   420→\t\t\t\t\tRuleId:    rule.Id,\n   421→\t\t\t\t\tVariantId: variant.Id,\n   422→\t\t\t\t\tCreatedAt: ss.now,\n   423→\t\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt: ss.now,\n   424→\t\t\t\t})\n   425→\n   426→\t\t\t\tevalDists[evalRule.ID] = append(evalDists[evalRule.ID], &storage.EvaluationDistribution{\n   427→\t\t\t\t\tID:                id,\n   428→\t\t\t\t\tRollout:           d.Rollout,\n   429→\t\t\t\t\tVariantID:         variant.Id,\n   430→\t\t\t\t\tVariantKey:        variant.Key,\n   431→\t\t\t\t\tVariantAttachment: variant.Attachment,\n   432→\t\t\t\t})\n   433→\t\t\t}\n   434→\n   435→\t\t\tns.rules[rule.Id] = rule\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\n   438→\t\tns.evalRules[f.Key] = evalRules\n   439→\n   440→\t\tevalRollouts := make([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, 0, len(f.Rollouts))\n   441→\t\tfor i, rollout := range f.Rollouts {\n   442→\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n   443→\t\t\ts := &storage.EvaluationRollout{\n   444→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   445→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   446→\t\t\t}\n   447→\n   448→\t\t\tflagRollout := &flipt.Rollout{\n   449→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   450→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   451→\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n   452→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   453→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   454→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   455→\t\t\t}\n   456→\n   457→\t\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n   458→\t\t\t\ts.Threshold = &storage.RolloutThreshold{\n   459→\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n   460→\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n   461→\t\t\t\t}\n   462→\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_THRESHOLD_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n   463→\n   464→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n   465→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Threshold{\n   466→\t\t\t\t\tThreshold: &flipt.RolloutThreshold{\n   467→\t\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n   468→\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n   469→\t\t\t\t\t},\n   470→\t\t\t\t}\n   471→\t\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n   472→\t\t\t\tvar (\n   473→\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n   474→\t\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n   475→\t\t\t\t)\n   476→\n   477→\t\t\t\tif rollout.Segment.Key != \"\" {\n   478→\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Key)\n   479→\t\t\t\t} else if len(rollout.Segment.Keys) > 0 {\n   480→\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Keys...)\n   481→\t\t\t\t}\n   482→\n   483→\t\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n   484→\t\t\t\t\tsegment, ok := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n   485→\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   486→\t\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n   487→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   488→\n   489→\t\t\t\t\tconstraints := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n   490→\t\t\t\t\tfor _, c := range segment.Constraints {\n   491→\t\t\t\t\t\tconstraints = append(constraints, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n   492→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: c.Operator,\n   493→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: c.Property,\n   494→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     c.Type,\n   495→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    c.Value,\n   496→\t\t\t\t\t\t})\n   497→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   498→\n   499→\t\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n   500→\t\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n   501→\t\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n   502→\t\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: constraints,\n   503→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   504→\t\t\t\t}\n   505→\n   506→\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[rollout.Segment.Operator]\n   507→\n   508→\t\t\t\ts.Segment = &storage.RolloutSegment{\n   509→\t\t\t\t\tSegments:        segments,\n   510→\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n   511→\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n   512→\t\t\t\t}\n   513→\n   514→\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_SEGMENT_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n   515→\n   516→\t\t\t\tfrs := &flipt.RolloutSegment{\n   517→\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n   518→\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n   519→\t\t\t\t}\n   520→\n   521→\t\t\t\tif len(segmentKeys) == 1 {\n   522→\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKey = segmentKeys[0]\n   523→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   524→\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n   525→\t\t\t\t}\n   526→\n   527→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n   528→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Segment{\n   529→\t\t\t\t\tSegment: frs,\n   530→\t\t\t\t}\n   531→\t\t\t}\n   532→\n   533→\t\t\tns.rollouts[flagRollout.Id] = flagRollout\n   534→\n   535→\t\t\tevalRollouts = append(evalRollouts, s)\n   536→\t\t}\n   537→\n   538→\t\tns.evalRollouts[f.Key] = evalRollouts\n   539→\t}\n   540→\n   541→\tss.ns[doc.Namespace] = ns\n   542→\n   543→\tss.evalDists = evalDists\n   544→\n   545→\treturn nil\n   546→}\n   547→\n   548→func (ss Snapshot) String() string {\n   549→\treturn \"snapshot\"\n   550→}\n   551→\n   552→func (ss *Snapshot) GetRule(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest, id string) (rule *flipt.Rule, _ error) {\n   553→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n   554→\tif err != nil {\n   555→\t\treturn nil, err\n   556→\t}\n   557→\n   558→\tvar ok bool\n   559→\trule, ok = ns.rules[id]\n   560→\tif !ok {\n   561→\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(`rule \"%s/%s\"`, p.Namespace(), id)\n   562→\t}\n   563→\n   564→\treturn rule, nil\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→func (ss *Snapshot) ListRules(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ResourceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Rule], _ error) {\n   568→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n   569→\tif err != nil {\n   570→\t\treturn set, err\n   571→\t}\n   572→\n   573→\trules := make([]*flipt.Rule, 0, len(ns.rules))\n   574→\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n   575→\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Predicate.Key {\n   576→\t\t\trules = append(rules, rule)\n   577→\t\t}\n   578→\t}\n   579→\n   580→\treturn paginate(req.QueryParams, func(i, j int) bool {\n   581→\t\treturn rules[i].Rank < rules[j].Rank\n   582→\t}, rules...)\n   583→}\n   584→\n   585→func (ss *Snapshot) CountRules(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n   586→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n   587→\tif err != nil {\n   588→\t\treturn 0, err\n   589→\t}\n   590→\n   591→\tvar count uint64 = 0\n   592→\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n   593→\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Key {\n   594→\t\t\tcount += 1\n   595→\t\t}\n   596→\t}\n   597→\n   598→\treturn count, nil\n   599→}\n   600→\n   601→func (ss *Snapshot) GetSegment(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Segment, error) {\n   602→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n   603→\tif err != nil {\n   604→\t\treturn nil, err\n 613→}\n   614→\n   615→func (ss *Snapshot) ListSegments(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.NamespaceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Segment], err error) {\n   616→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n   617→\tif err != nil {\n   618→\t\treturn set, err\n   619→\t}\n   620→\n   621→\tsegments := make([]*flipt.Segment, 0, len(ns.segments))\n   622→\tfor segments[i].Key < segments[j].Key\n   628→\t}, segments...)\n   629→}\n   630→\n   631→func (ss *Snapshot) CountSegments(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n (ss *Snapshot) GetNamespace(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (*flipt.Namespace, error) {\n   641→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n   642→\tif err != nil {\n   643→\t\treturn nil, err\n   644→\t}\n   645→\n   646→\treturn ns.resource, nil\n   647→}\n   648→\n   649→func (ss *Snapshot) ListNamespaces(ctx context.Context, req 659→\n   660→func (ss *Snapshot) CountNamespaces(ctx context.Context, _ storage.ReferenceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n   661→\treturn uint64(len(ss.ns)), nil\n   662→}\n   663→\n   664→func (ss *Snapshot) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {\n   665→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n   666→\tif err != nil {\n   667→\t\treturn nil, 676→}\n   677→\n   678→func (ss *Snapshot) ListFlags(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.NamespaceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Flag], err error) {\n   679→\tns, err := 691→\t}, flags...)\n   692→}\n   693→\n   694→func (ss *Snapshot) CountFlags(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n   695→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error) {\n   704→\tns, ok := ss.ns[flag.Namespace()]\n   705→\tif !ok {\n   706→\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(\"namespace %q\", 714→\treturn rules, nil\n   715→}\n   716→\n   717→func (ss *Snapshot) GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, rule storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error) {\n   718→\tdists, ok := ss.evalDists[rule.ID]\n   719→\tif !ok {\n   720→\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(\"rule %q\", rule.ID)\n   721→\t}\n   722→\n   723→\treturn dists, nil\n   724→}\n   725→\n
